I didn't know this singer until the summer of 2020. That's when I heard Kings & Queens and Sweet but Psycho through twitter and Tik Tok. Neither of these songs did anything for me.  I can admit I am pretentious with pop music, so I kind of stuck my nose up to her. All the music I knew of hers wasn't fresh. Her damn haircut just added fuel to the fire. I never gave her much of a chance. However, I finally did a listen through of Heaven & Hell today and wow. What an album. It is a fun, sugary-plastic coated, nostalgia-packed mix tape of old melodies turned into something new. It has like 12 tracks and maybe 3 of them are average. For a first record, Ava delivered! Some have called her shallow or unoriginal, but this song defies that for me. It is so intimate and personal. I will be streaming!!
